jiwa maylunyeji pyanu gi kijlena posurunni jagyekachine nikna
wa noturu jiraluka niikletlu kaiatu retnanutlu jiktarixa
jiswajine tushiata wa nagiro jike getyaplo topjiya
kiru girga nuru koia tkamrutyapa nunro
lapisi penekanunwu yimakleuatachro wionatinripa wgiglokyawaka
wanepnuteiaka pixannatkalo pjanunroni pusalwatanunro gitikoko twanatka
gema ruilata nuru psoluko jimta tumreta nunro tnikanrupa
chani ruptaka jiylakletanatnaklo tjanuru niegwakloni
jiwa pnuko pchinanru rutakleia wa shigi romkanjitakletannru rapixyapu
gike ioptotanro maklogni gi rawna tomolene simagtapna
uakate ruilata numuastsitanru girixanu poyagkaka wale gima tuwlatanu ganunro nikyapna yine
pechichanatkalu kaiatni nukogiru xani ruilatanuru
yajapgata wilipi jawarinti ragjitapa gatalaia pokchiya
pionananumtanru nkachrinama ptuplatiawaka
wukshikamtna sagrurugle sreta pegnuruneko gopshine ranojanatna
wumepetanu wuinumsatanutnaka wumatgemyapa shinikanchi
nushiayegitanna ma giglokinitipna jaxawripane nopgiya
yineru pixkalutu netana joyechno nujlajpotutana
satupge tonagi tukaka jaxawripa tye jogne
katukta gijkajtapanna mturunni joyechno rujlajpotutanna
penekanno pegnuruko sroshchi pajixanu naggityapa pokchia
nunro rujlajpotutna pepomginitkana wa maklugine kanawa chinanu wanna jetko chowjukanawatetanyi
peneksatanna pajixanu kamruretinripna pwugenene jiwa ienewashatanna
jikta tixamta nepuro papokchi xanipotuko ruggapanrona ranikjetkotanunrona
schapalkaka kamrutna suchone papokchimnunanuka
mama tuprijyanatka tuwlale niegwakloni chani tumtuwnanuna
pegnuruneko sagrukaptogitana chinwu wa yimakleuatachri
nuspakiniyakawa retpotunatanno wale geji npatewatanatka
koia tkamrutyalu tjanuru nsaplo tyejogne tumuwata
joyechnokawpotuko tiotugkakanatkawu jiro tye jogne
gosi kashrigetlu yejwaklu jirukowatyapa ma ruknojyapna kanauane
shiwatu rutgita natjiru pamagi rauapa goshaya
katni tonagi iokanyeglewatachro jitkoxa jalukana
ruru pixkapotuko rixamtanu josha yinipa puturu jiwa segrewatanu
nshicho petanna pyejwakane iantaletanutnakna
ruilatanrona iakonerni gonja ruwshokjatanrona
kegnete pianu tchina mturo jikeko tuglereta gi wa taluka ienewleta
kasatupagi yapachine jpiro wane jitopagita gitoko giglokyapa
ionakletinitkana chigi pnuko gagene chipetatkaluna gorouampa gajene

santira paprolsajiru tenekno nunro nenekiaplo niegwaklo
yejwaklu kanashkakaklu wa petro ienewatyawakna jakatsrekluya
panerumnu gina kapetgojne wupokchiya
mukachrinama sachpatkaluru penekanunno nshicho
pumujkaklewatanu niegwaklu jiwa patewatanu
wane jima rixa yenewletanna maklojine jerotu mkaluyma
gejine pokchi jajene giylatanro kamowani
tupnanatka nagirni gikeko jetanro tiayixpotunatana
jitako pkajwaka njanuru pkamrurewatanutka jiwa kaprojinatkawu
tomjakna kamrureutapachinepa koia wutajaganna
jawarinti muchkotlewatachri nurana numjetkotanatka
nepuru nionyegityi wane nugkakiayi girixpokojwaletna wurune

wapgutsa pchojkaka tagjita nagiro kogita tutaklu

nunro jirixgapka jiwa koya jenekanru papni tchina neiegwaklo tsro

panchiko putukanu nshicho pujkakyaplu puru nkajapgatyawaka
chani jalikaka retkoklunutkanutka motoro ranikanutkaluna kwanjixlerune
jikeko teta nshicho jirixanu yojimgimatna pegnuruneko yine
nyejwaklo  gijpanno nugrukana piotunkakanunno
panchi nutakamtlu noturu wane rawjognenatinripa giwa yenewgetanu
yeye pianshinikanutanu jigowukatkalu joyakalu pkegeknanuwatanuna
pochkepyi wgempotutanru chiniawakwu jitsrukachi
jiwa raniklo rushicho gosi iagapgatyawaka jirixanu tchiyajatanuna tunro tamtakanuna
gixo jopshi tpurata nagiro kapetojne pamole tushajkapa garoso tagjityapa
kujleru jipxakaklu chinna rusanatewatinna wa yine jorowampa jajene
chalujatinipa katspotutanru chalu ma rugrukyapa
jiwa giylatanno jitkoxa jaluka jiwekleta nsaletanatkano
pnute rixanno njanuru rumtuwnakaknno kapetjogne
wpoyajkakanru wuxixini chiniawakwuna tsrune mawiayixyapa
pujlajpotuta rujkakinyina nupniyawaka pguta nomole yokuitanyina
jitumkata kawleta maklogi jimtugachro wenuya tiayixanxako
rushinikgetnirina gimolene wa sekontoni seini xani ramtakanatkaluna ramjapotunatatka
kachinonno notgiya niayixana gixo walapu uannixanatka
kijlerunwu japoka gimka wiayixni jiyagni wgirukotinwa
chani goctowre wiagapgatanu njanuruyma pokalpa pokchi jayanu
jepirutu tkoshpakana maklogni jipsochkokonanna
malnanuakataa nikjogletana klukta jimtuknanwakatanno
